\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
This \mbox{\hyperlink{class_look_and_feel}{Look\+And\+Feel}} subclass implements the juce style from around 2008-\/12.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{drawBevel@{drawBevel}!LookAndFeel\_V2@{LookAndFeel\_V2}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawBevel()}{drawBevel()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Look\+And\+Feel\+\_\+\+V2\+::draw\+Bevel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} \&}]{,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{y,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{bevel\+Thickness,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_colour}{Colour}} \&}]{top\+Left\+Colour = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_colours_a62eff4c03f8f8e0805bc5d4e47cf24ec}{Colours\+::white}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_colour}{Colour}} \&}]{bottom\+Right\+Colour = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_colours_ab5f46ac613c2b717ac885b7cf995ffc6}{Colours\+::black}}},  }\item[{bool}]{use\+Gradient = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}},  }\item[{bool}]{sharp\+Edge\+On\+Outside = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Draws a 3D raised (or indented) bevel using two colours.

The bevel is drawn inside the given rectangle, and greater bevel thicknesses extend inwards.

The top-\/left colour is used for the top-\/ and left-\/hand edges of the bevel; the bottom-\/right colour is used for the bottom-\/ and right-\/hand edges.

If use\+Gradient is true, then the bevel fades out to make it look more curved and less angular. If sharp\+Edge\+On\+Outside is true, the outside of the bevel is sharp, and it fades towards the centre; if sharp\+Edge\+On\+Outside is false, then the centre edges are sharp and it fades towards the outside. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_look_and_feel___v2_a28f4d0d531043e90e8b0884eaa642d20}\label{class_look_and_feel___v2_a28f4d0d531043e90e8b0884eaa642d20}}

\index{LookAndFeel\_V2@{LookAndFeel\_V2}!drawProgressBar@{drawProgressBar}}
\index{drawProgressBar@{drawProgressBar}!LookAndFeel\_V2@{LookAndFeel\_V2}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawProgressBar()}{drawProgressBar()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Look\+And\+Feel\+\_\+\+V2\+::draw\+Progress\+Bar (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} \&}]{,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_progress_bar}{Progress\+Bar}} \&}]{,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{height,  }\item[{double}]{progress,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_string}{String}} \&}]{text\+To\+Show }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Draws a progress bar.

If the progress value is less than 0 or greater than 1.\+0, this should draw a spinning bar that fills the whole space (i.\+e. to say that the app is still busy but the progress isn\textquotesingle{}t known). It can use the current time as a basis for playing an animation.

(Used by progress bars in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_alert_window}{Alert\+Window}}). 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_progress_bar_1_1_look_and_feel_methods_a122aff7bf66df1a32b8d1f3973415e0f}{Progress\+Bar\+::\+Look\+And\+Feel\+Methods}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawScrollbar()}{drawScrollbar()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Look\+And\+Feel\+\_\+\+V2\+::draw\+Scrollbar (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} \&}]{g,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_scroll_bar}{Scroll\+Bar}} \&}]{scrollbar,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{y,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{height,  }\item[{bool}]{is\+Scrollbar\+Vertical,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{thumb\+Start\+Position,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{thumb\+Size,  }\item[{bool}]{is\+Mouse\+Over,  }\item[{bool}]{is\+Mouse\+Down }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Draws the thumb area of a scrollbar.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em g} & the context to draw into \\
\hline
{\em scrollbar} & the bar itself \\
\hline
{\em x} & the x position of the left edge of the thumb area to draw in \\
\hline
{\em y} & the y position of the top edge of the thumb area to draw in \\
\hline
{\em width} & the width of the thumb area to draw in \\
\hline
{\em height} & the height of the thumb area to draw in \\
\hline
{\em is\+Scrollbar\+Vertical} & true if it\textquotesingle{}s a vertical bar, false if horizontal \\
\hline
{\em thumb\+Start\+Position} & for vertical bars, the y coordinate of the top of the thumb, or its x position for horizontal bars \\
\hline
{\em thumb\+Size} & for vertical bars, the height of the thumb, or its width for horizontal bars. This may be 0 if the thumb shouldn\textquotesingle{}t be drawn. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Mouse\+Over} & whether the mouse is over the thumb area, also true if the mouse is currently dragging the thumb \\
\hline
{\em is\+Mouse\+Down} & whether the mouse is currently dragging the scrollbar \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_scroll_bar_1_1_look_and_feel_methods_ad096796eb73636308c4cdc884a2dc244}{Scroll\+Bar\+::\+Look\+And\+Feel\+Methods}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_look_and_feel___v2_afc97f2f47828c1bdb2fd1ead4d1d3b8d}\label{class_look_and_feel___v2_afc97f2f47828c1bdb2fd1ead4d1d3b8d}} 
\index{LookAndFeel\_V2@{LookAndFeel\_V2}!drawScrollbarButton@{drawScrollbarButton}}
\index{drawScrollbarButton@{drawScrollbarButton}!LookAndFeel\_V2@{LookAndFeel\_V2}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawScrollbarButton()}{drawScrollbarButton()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Look\+And\+Feel\+\_\+\+V2\+::draw\+Scrollbar\+Button (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} \&}]{g,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_scroll_bar}{Scroll\+Bar}} \&}]{scrollbar,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{button\+Direction,  }\item[{bool}]{is\+Scrollbar\+Vertical,  }\item[{bool}]{is\+Mouse\+Over\+Button,  }\item[{bool}]{is\+Button\+Down }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Draws one of the buttons on a scrollbar.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em g} & the context to draw into \\
\hline
{\em scrollbar} & the bar itself \\
\hline
{\em width} & the width of the button \\
\hline
{\em height} & the height of the button \\
\hline
{\em button\+Direction} & the direction of the button, where 0 = up, 1 = right, 2 = down, 3 = left \\
\hline
{\em is\+Scrollbar\+Vertical} & true if it\textquotesingle{}s a vertical bar, false if horizontal \\
\hline
{\em is\+Mouse\+Over\+Button} & whether the mouse is currently over the button (also true if it\textquotesingle{}s held down) \\
\hline
{\em is\+Button\+Down} & whether the mouse button\textquotesingle{}s held down \\
